                        "import requests\nimport time\nimport threading\nfrom collections import defaultdict\nfrom tabulate import tabulate\n\n# Constants for GraphQL endpoints\nGRAPHQL_ENDPOINTS = {\n    'Uniswap': 'https://api.thegraph.com/subgraphs/name/uniswap/uniswap-v2',\n    'PancakeSwap': 'https://bsc.streamingfast.io/subgraphs/name/pancakeswap/exchange-v2',\n    'Sushiswap': 'https://api.thegraph.com/subgraphs/name/sushiswap/exchange',\n}\n\n# Number of tokens to fetch from each DEX (for demo purposes)\nTOKENS_PER_DEX = 50\n\ndef fetch_token_prices(exchange_name, endpoint):\n    \"\"\"\n    Fetch tokens and their prices from the given DEX GraphQL endpoint.\n    Returns a dict: {token_address: {'symbol': ..., 'name': ..., 'price': ...}}\n    \"\"\"\n    # Query top tokens by volume, getting their price in USD\n    query = \"\"\"\n    {\n      pairs(first: %d, orderBy: volumeUSD, orderDirection: desc) {\n        token0 {\n          id\n          symbol\n          name\n        }\n        token1 {\n          id\n          symbol\n          name\n        }\n        reserveUSD\n        token0Price\n        token1Price\n      }\n    }\n    \"\"\" % TOKENS_PER_DEX\n\n    try:\n        response = requests.post(endpoint, json={'query': query}, timeout=10)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        data = response.json()\n        pairs = data['data']['pairs']\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"[{exchange_name}] Error fetching data: {e}\")\n        return {}\n\n    tokens = {}\n    for pair in pairs:\n        # For each token in the pair, estimate its price in USD\n        # We use reserveUSD and token price ratios to estimate\n        reserveUSD = float(pair['reserveUSD']) if pair['reserveUSD'] else 0.0\n        # For token0\n        token0 = pair['token0']\n        token0_price = float(pair['token0Price']) if pair['token0Price'] else 0.0\n        # For token1\n        token1 = pair['token1']\n        token1_price = float(pair['token1Price']) if pair['token1Price'] else 0.0\n\n        # For estimation, take reserveUSD / 2 as each token's USD value in the pair\n        # This is a simplification, but works for most pairs\n        if token0['id'] not in tokens and token0_price > 0:\n            tokens[token0['id']] = {\n                'symbol': token0['symbol'],\n                'name': token0['name'],\n                'price': reserveUSD / 2 / token0_price if token0_price else 0.0\n            }\n        if token1['id'] not in tokens and token1_price > 0:\n            tokens[token1['id']] = {\n                'symbol': token1['symbol'],\n                'name': token1['name'],\n                'price': reserveUSD / 2 / token1_price if token1_price else 0.0\n            }\n    return tokens\n\ndef aggregate_tokens():\n    \"\"\"\n    Fetch tokens from all DEXes and aggregate prices for tokens available on at least two exchanges.\n    Returns:\n        token_data: dict of {token_address: {'symbol': ..., 'name': ..., 'prices': {exchange: price}}}\n    \"\"\"\n    dex_tokens = {}\n    for dex, endpoint in GRAPHQL_ENDPOINTS.items():\n        dex_tokens[dex] = fetch_token_prices(dex, endpoint)\n\n    # Aggregate tokens by address\n    token_data = defaultdict(lambda: {'symbol': '', 'name': '', 'prices': {}})\n    for dex, tokens in dex_tokens.items():\n        for addr, info in tokens.items():\n            token_data[addr]['symbol'] = info['symbol']\n            token_data[addr]['name'] = info['name']\n            token_data[addr]['prices'][dex] = info['price']\n\n    # Filter tokens present on at least two exchanges\n    filtered = {addr: data for addr, data in token_data.items() if len(data['prices']) >= 2}\n    return filtered\n\ndef analyze_tokens(token_data):\n    \"\"\"\n    Analyze tokens for price differences > 1.8% between exchanges.\n    Returns a list of dicts with relevant info for dashboard.\n    \"\"\"\n    results = []\n    for addr, data in token_data.items():\n        prices = data['prices']\n        price_list = [(dex, price) for dex, price in prices.items() if price > 0]\n        if len(price_list) < 2:\n            continue\n        price_list.sort(key=lambda x: x[1])\n        lowest = price_list[0]\n        highest = price_list[-1]\n        if lowest[1] == 0:\n            continue\n        diff_percent = ((highest[1] - lowest[1]) / lowest[1]) * 100\n        if diff_percent > 1.8:\n            results.append({\n                'Name': data['name'],\n                'Symbol': data['symbol'],\n                'Address': addr,\n                'Lowest Exchange': lowest[0],\n                'Lowest Price': f\"${lowest[1]:.4f}\",\n                'Highest Exchange': highest[0],\n                'Highest Price': f\"${highest[1]:.4f}\",\n                'Diff (%)': f\"{diff_percent:.2f}%\"\n            })\n    return results\n\ndef display_dashboard(results):\n    \"\"\"\n    Display the results in a table format.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not results:\n        print(\"No tokens found with price difference > 1.8% on at least two exchanges.\")\n        return\n    headers = [\"Name\", \"Symbol\", \"Address\", \"Lowest Exchange\", \"Lowest Price\",\n               \"Highest Exchange\", \"Highest Price\", \"Diff (%)\"]\n    print(tabulate(results, headers=headers, tablefmt=\"grid\"))\n\ndef monitor_loop():\n    \"\"\"\n    Main monitoring loop: fetch, analyze, and display every second.\n    \"\"\"\n    while True:\n        print(\"\\033c\", end=\"\")  # Clear terminal\n        print(f\"--- Real-Time Token Price Arbitrage Monitor ---\")\n        print(f\"Fetching data from Uniswap, PancakeSwap, Sushiswap...\")\n        token_data = aggregate_tokens()\n        results = analyze_tokens(token_data)\n        display_dashboard(results)\n        print(f\"\\nUpdated: {time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\")\n        time.sleep(1)\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    try:\n        monitor_loop()\n    except KeyboardInterrupt:\n        print(\"\\nMonitoring stopped by user.\")",
                        "import requests\nimport threading\nimport time\nfrom flask import Flask, render_template_string\n\n# =========================\n# Configuration & Constants\n# =========================\n\nUPDATE_INTERVAL = 1  # seconds\nPRICE_DIFF_THRESHOLD = 0.018  # 1.8%\nSUPPORTED_EXCHANGES = {\n    'Uniswap': {\n        'chain': 'ethereum',\n        'graphql': 'https://api.thegraph.com/subgraphs/name/uniswap/uniswap-v2',\n    },\n    'Sushiswap': {\n        'chain': 'ethereum',\n        'graphql': 'https://api.thegraph.com/subgraphs/name/sushiswap/exchange',\n    },\n    'PancakeSwap': {\n        'chain': 'bsc',\n        'graphql': 'https://bsc.streamingfast.io/subgraphs/name/pancakeswap/exchange-v2',\n    }\n}\n\n# =========================\n# GraphQL Queries\n# =========================\n\nPAIR_QUERY = \"\"\"\n{\n  pairs(first: 50, orderBy: reserveUSD, orderDirection: desc) {\n    id\n    token0 {\n      id\n      symbol\n      name\n    }\n    token1 {\n      id\n      symbol\n      name\n    }\n    reserveUSD\n    token0Price\n    token1Price\n  }\n}\n\"\"\"\n\n# =========================\n# Data Fetching Functions\n# =========================\n\ndef fetch_pairs(exchange_name, graphql_url):\n    \"\"\"\n    Fetch top pairs from the given exchange's subgraph.\n    Returns: List of dicts with token info and price.\n    \"\"\"\n    try:\n        response = requests.post(graphql_url, json={'query': PAIR_QUERY}, timeout=10)\n        data = response.json()\n        pairs = data['data']['pairs']\n        tokens = []\n        for pair in pairs:\n            # For each token in the pair, get price in terms of the other token\n            # We'll use token0 as the base\n            tokens.append({\n                'exchange': exchange_name,\n                'token_address': pair['token0']['id'],\n                'token_symbol': pair['token0']['symbol'],\n                'token_name': pair['token0']['name'],\n                'price': float(pair['token1Price']),  # token0 price in token1\n                'pair_address': pair['id'],\n            })\n            tokens.append({\n                'exchange': exchange_name,\n                'token_address': pair['token1']['id'],\n                'token_symbol': pair['token1']['symbol'],\n                'token_name': pair['token1']['name'],\n                'price': float(pair['token0Price']),  # token1 price in token0\n                'pair_address': pair['id'],\n            })\n        return tokens\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Error fetching from {exchange_name}: {e}\")\n        return []\n\ndef aggregate_tokens():\n    \"\"\"\n    Fetch and aggregate token prices from all exchanges.\n    Returns: dict mapping token_address => { 'name', 'symbol', 'prices': {exchange: price} }\n    \"\"\"\n    all_tokens = {}\n    for exchange, info in SUPPORTED_EXCHANGES.items():\n        tokens = fetch_pairs(exchange, info['graphql'])\n        for t in tokens:\n            addr = t['token_address']\n            if addr not in all_tokens:\n                all_tokens[addr] = {\n                    'name': t['token_name'],\n                    'symbol': t['token_symbol'],\n                    'prices': {},\n                    'contract_address': addr\n                }\n            # Some tokens might appear in multiple pairs, keep lowest price for each exchange\n            prev_price = all_tokens[addr]['prices'].get(exchange)\n            if prev_price is None or t['price'] < prev_price:\n                all_tokens[addr]['prices'][exchange] = t['price']\n    return all_tokens\n\ndef analyze_tokens(all_tokens):\n    \"\"\"\n    Analyze tokens available on at least two exchanges, with price diff > threshold.\n    Returns: List of dicts with required info.\n    \"\"\"\n    result = []\n    for token in all_tokens.values():\n        prices = token['prices']\n        if len(prices) < 2:\n            continue  # Only interested in tokens on >=2 exchanges\n        # Find lowest and highest price exchanges\n        exchanges = list(prices.keys())\n        price_list = [(ex, prices[ex]) for ex in exchanges if prices[ex] > 0]\n        if len(price_list) < 2:\n            continue\n        price_list.sort(key=lambda x: x[1])\n        low_ex, low_price = price_list[0]\n        high_ex, high_price = price_list[-1]\n        if low_price == 0:\n            continue\n        price_diff = (high_price - low_price) / low_price\n        if price_diff > PRICE_DIFF_THRESHOLD:\n            result.append({\n                'name': token['name'],\n                'symbol': token['symbol'],\n                'contract_address': token['contract_address'],\n                'lowest_exchange': low_ex,\n                'lowest_price': low_price,\n                'highest_exchange': high_ex,\n                'highest_price': high_price,\n                'price_diff_percent': price_diff * 100,\n            })\n    return result\n\n# =========================\n# Real-Time Data Storage\n# =========================\n\nlatest_results = []\nlock = threading.Lock()\n\ndef update_data():\n    \"\"\"\n    Periodically fetch and analyze token data.\n    \"\"\"\n    global latest_results\n    while True:\n        all_tokens = aggregate_tokens()\n        results = analyze_tokens(all_tokens)\n        with lock:\n            latest_results = results\n        time.sleep(UPDATE_INTERVAL)\n\n# =========================\n# Flask Dashboard\n# =========================\n\napp = Flask(__name__)\n\nDASHBOARD_HTML = \"\"\"\n<!DOCTYPE html>\n<html>\n<head>\n    <title>DEX Token Price Monitor</title>\n    <meta http-equiv=\"refresh\" content=\"1\">\n    <style>\n        body { font-family: Arial, sans-serif; margin: 20px; }\n        table { border-collapse: color: red; }\n    </style>\n</head>\n<body>\n    <h2>DEX Token Price Monitor</h2>\n    <p>Tokens listed on at least two exchanges with price difference &gt; 1.8%</p>\n    <table>\n        <tr>\n            <th>Name</th>\n            <th>Symbol</th>\n            <th>Contract Address</th>\n            <th>Lowest Price Exchange</th>\n            <th>Lowest Price</th>\n            <th>Highest Price Exchange</th>\n            <th>Highest Price</th>\n            <th>Price Diff (%)</th>\n        </tr>\n        {% for token in tokens %}\n        <tr>\n            <td>{{ token.name }}</td>\n            <td>{{ token.symbol }}</td>\n            <td><a href=\"https://etherscan.io/token/{{ token.contract_address }}\" target=\"_blank\">{{ token.contract_address[:10] }}...</a></td>\n            <td class=\"low\">{{ token.lowest_exchange }}</td>\n            <td class=\"low\">{{ \"%.6f\"|format(token.lowest_price) }}</td>\n            <td class=\"high\">{{ token.highest_exchange }}</td>\n            <td class=\"high\">{{ \"%.6f\"|format(token.highest_price) }}</td>\n            <td>{{ \"%.2f\"|format(token.price_diff_percent) }}</td>\n        </tr>\n        {% endfor %}\n    </table>\n    <p>Last updated: {{ update_time }}</p>\n</body>\n</html>\n\"\"\"\n\n@app.route('/')\ndef dashboard():\n    with lock:\n        tokens = latest_results.copy()\n    update_time = time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S', time.localtime())\n    return render_template_string(DASHBOARD_HTML, tokens=tokens, update_time=update_time)\n\n# =========================\n# Main Entrypoint\n#                         "import unittest\nfrom unittest.mock import patch, MagicMock\nfrom collections import defaultdict\n\n# Import functions to test from the original code\n# For this test script, we assume the code above is in a module named 'dex_monitor'\n# If the code is in the same file, you can remove the import and use the functions directly\n\n# For demonstration, we redefine the functions here that we want to test\n# In your actual test environment, import them from the module\n\n# --- Begin: Functions to test (copied from user code, but without Flask/threading/network) ---\n\nTOP_N_PAIRS = 50\n\ndef analyze_tokens(tokens_multi_dex):\n    \"\"\"Analyze tokens for price differences >1.8% and return dashboard data.\"\"\"\n    dashboard_rows = []\n    for token_addr, pairs in tokens_multi_dex.items():\n        prices = [(pair['dex'], pair['price']) for pair in pairs]\n        prices_sorted = sorted(prices, key=lambda x: x[1])\n        lowest = prices_sorted[0]\n        highest = prices_sorted[-1]\n        # Sort by price difference descending\n    dashboard_rows.sort(key=lambda x: x['price_diff_pct'], reverse=True)\n    return dashboard_rows\n\ndef aggregate_token_data():\n    \"\"\"Fetch data from all DEXs and aggregate by token address.\"\"\"\n    dex_fetchers = [\n        fetch_pairs_uniswap,\n        fetch_pairs_pancakeswap,\n        fetch_pairs_sushiswap\n    ]\n    all_pairs = []\n    for fetcher in dex_fetchers:\n        try:\n            pairs = fetcher()\n            all_pairs.extend(pairs)\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"Error fetching from DEX: {e}\")\n\n    # Aggregate by token address\n    tokens = defaultdict(list)\n    for pair in all_pairs:\n        tokens[pair['token_address']].append(pair)\n\n    # Only keep tokens that are present on at least two DEXs\n    tokens_multi_dex = {addr: pairs for addr, pairs in tokens.items() if len(pairs) >= 2}\n    return tokens_multi_dex\n\n# The fetch_pairs_* functions will be mocked in tests\n\n# --- End: Functions to test ---\n\nclass TestDexMonitor(unittest.TestCase):\n\n    def setUp(self):\n        # >1.8% diff from Uniswap\n                'dex': 'PancakeSwap'\n            },\n            {\n                'token_address': '0xTokenC',\n                'token_symbol': 'TKC',\n                'token_name': 'TokenC',\n                'pair_address': '0xPairC2',\n                'price': 5.0,\n                'dex': 'PancakeSwap'\n            },\n        ]\n        self.mock_pairs_sushiswap = [\n            {\n                'token_address': '0xTokenA',\n                'token_symbol': 'TKA',\n                'token_name': 'TokenA',\n                'pair_address': '0xPairA3',\n                'price': 11.0,  # Set up mocks\n        mock_uni.return_value = self.mock_pairs_uniswap\n        mock_pancake.return_value = self.mock_pairs_pancakeswap\n        mock_sushi.return_value = self.mock_pairs_sushiswap\n\n        tokens_multi_dex = aggregate_token_data()\n        # TokenA appears on all 3 DEXs\n        # TokenB appears on 2 DEXs\n        # TokenC only on PancakeSwap\n        # TokenD only on Sushiswap\n\n        self.assertIn('0xTokenA', tokens_multi_dex)\n        self.assertIn('0xTokenB', tokens_multi_dex)\n        self.assertNotIn('0xTokenC', tokens_multi_dex)\n        self.assertNotIn('0xTokenD', tokens_multi_dex)\n        self.assertEqual(len(tokens_multi_dex['0xTokenA']), 3)\n        self.assertEqual(len(tokens_multi_dex['0xTokenB']), 2)\n\n    def test_analyze_tokens_basic(self):\n        # TokenA: lowest=10.0, highest=11.0, diff=10%\n        # TokenB: lowest=20.0, highest=21.0, diff=5%\n        self.assertEqual(len(dashboard), 2)\n        tokenA_row = next(row for row in dashboard if row['token_symbol'] == 'TKA')\n        tokenB_row = next(row for row in dashboard if row['token_symbol'] == 'TKB')\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(tokenA_row['lowest_price'], 10.0)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(tokenA_row['highest_price'], 11.0)\n        self.assertEqual(tokenA_row['lowest_dex'], 'Uniswap')\n        self.assertEqual(tokenA_row['highest_dex'], 'Sushiswap')\n        self.assertGreater(tokenA_row['price_diff_pct'], 1.8)\n\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(tokenB_row['lowest_price'], 20.0)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(tokenB_row['highest_price'], 21.0)\n        self.assertEqual(tokenB_row['lowest_dex'], 'Uniswap')\n        self.assertEqual(tokenB_row['highest_dex'], 'PancakeSwap')\n        self.assertGreater(tokenB_row['price_diff_pct'], 1.8)\n\n    def test_analyze_tokens_excludes_small_diff(self):\n        # diff = 5%\n        }\n        dashboard = analyze_tokens(tokens_multi_dex)\n        # Only TokenB should be included\n        self.assertEqual(len(dashboard), 1)\n        self.assertEqual(dashboard[0]['token_symbol'], 'TKB')\n\n    def test_analyze_tokens_zero_price(self):\n        #        # tokenA: prices 1.8, 2.0, 2.2; diff = (2.2-1.8)/1.8*100 = 22.22% > 1.8%\n        # tokenC: prices 4.0, 4.1; diff = (4.1-4.0)/4.0*100 = 2.5% > 1.8%\n        self.assertEqual(len(dashboard_rows), 2)\n        tokenA_row = next(row for row in dashboard_rows if row['token_symbol'] == 'TKNA')\n        tokenC_row = next(row for row in dashboard_rows if self.assertEqual(tokenA_row['lowest_dex'], 'Sushiswap')\n        self.assertEqual(tokenA_row['highest_dex'], 'PancakeSwap')\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(tokenA_row['price_diff_pct'], 22.22, places=2)\n        self.assertEqual(tokenC_row['lowest_price'], 4.0)\n        self.assertEqual(tokenC_row['highest_price'], 4.1)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(tokenC_row['price_diff_pct'], 2.5, places=2)\n\n    def test_analyze_tokens_edge_cases(self):\n        # Case: price difference exactly 1.8% should NOT be included\n        tokens_multi_dex = {\n            'tokenX': [\n ]\n        }\n        dashboard_rows = analyze_tokens(tokens_multi_dex)\n        # (10.18-10.0)/10.0*100 = 1.8%\n        self.assertEqual(len(dashboard_rows), 0)\n\n        # Case: lowest price is for DEX queries\n# -------------------------------\n\ndef fetch_pairs_generic(dex_name):\n    \"\"\"\n    Generic function to fetch token pairs and prices from a DEX using TheGraph.\n    Returns a list of dicts with token info and price.\n    \"\"\"\n    endpoint = DEX_ENDPOINTS[dex_name]\n    query = '''\n    {\n      pairs(first: %d, orderBy: reserveUSD, orderDirection: desc) {\n        id\n        token0 { id symbol name }\n        token1 { id symbol name }\n        reserveUSD\n        token0Price\n        token1Price\n      }\n    }\n    ''' % TOP_N_PAIRS\n    try:\n        resp = lowest[1] == 0:\n            continue\n        price_diff_pct = ((highest[1] - lowest[1]) / lowest[1]) * 100\n        if price_diff_pct > 1.8:\n            dashboard_rows.append({\n                         "import time\nimport threading\nimport requests\nfrom collections import defaultdict\nfrom flask import Flask, render_template_string\n\n# --- Constants for GraphQL endpoints of the DEXs ---\nDEX_ENDPOINTS = {\n    'Uniswap': 'https://api.thegraph.com/subgraphs/name/uniswap/uniswap-v2',\n    'PancakeSwap': 'https://bsc.streamingfast.io/subgraphs/name/pancakeswap/exchange-v2',\n    'Sushiswap': 'https://api.thegraph.com/subgraphs/name/sushiswap/exchange',\n}\n\n# Number of top pairs to fetch from each DEX\nTOP_N_PAIRS = 50\n\n# Flask app setup\napp = Flask(__name__)\n\n# Shared data structure for dashboard\ndashboard_data = []\n\ndef fetch_pairs_from_dex(dex_name, endpoint):\n    \"\"\"\n    Generic function to fetch token pairs and prices from a DEX via TheGraph.\n    Returns a list of dicts with token info and price.\n    \"\"\"\n    query = '''\n    {\n      pairs(first: %d, orderBy: reserveUSD, orderDirection: desc) {\n        id\n        token0 { id symbol name }\n        token1 { id symbol name }\n        reserveUSD\n        token0Price\n        token1Price\n      }\n    }\n    ''' % TOP_N_PAIRS\n    try:\n        resp = requests.post(endpoint, json={'query': query}, timeout=10)\n        resp.raise_for_status()\n        data = resp.json()\n        pairs = []\n        for pair in data['data']['pairs']:\n            # Use token0 as base, price = token1Price (token0 in terms of token1)\n            pairs.append({\n                'token_address': pair['token0']['id'],\n                'token_symbol': pair['token0']['symbol'],\n                'token_name': pair['token0']['name'],\n                'pair_address': pair['id'],\n                'price':   continue  # Need at least two valid prices\n\n        prices_sorted = sorted(prices, key=lambda x: x[1])\n        lowest = prices_sorted[0]\n        highest = prices_sorted[-1]\n\n        if lowest[1] == 0:\n            continue  # Avoid division by zero\n\n        price_diff_pct = ((highest[1] - lowest[1]) / lowest[1]) * 100\n        if price_diff_pct > 1.8:\n      token0 { id symbol name }\n        token1 { id symbol name }\n        reserveUSD\n        token0Price\n        token1Price\n      }\n    }\n    ''' % TOP_N_PAIRS\n    try:\n        resp = lowest = prices_sorted[0]\n        highest = prices_sorted[-1]\n        if lowest[1] == 0:\n            continue\n        price_diff_pct = ((highest[1] - lowest[1]) / lowest[1]) * 100\n        if price_diff_pct > 1.8:\n            dashboard_rows.append({\n                'token_name': pairs[0]['token_name'],\n                'token_symbol': pairs[0]['token_symbol'],\n self.assertEqual(pairs[0]['dex'], 'Uniswap')\n\n    @patch('requests.post')\n    def test_fetch_pairs_generic_handles_invalid_price(self, mock_post):\n        # Arrange\n        mock_resp =                         "import unittest\nfrom unittest.mock import patch, MagicMock\nfrom collections import defaultdict\n\n# Import functions/classes from the code to test\n# For this script, we assume the code above is in the same file or imported appropriately.\n# We'll re-define only the functions we need for testing context.\n\n# Copy-paste the relevant functions for testing (simulate import)\ndef analyze_tokens(tokens_multi_dex):\n    dashboard_rows = []\n    for token_addr, pairs in tokens_multi_dex.items():\n        prices = [(pair['dex'], pair['price']) for pair in pairs if pair['price'] > 0]\n        if len(prices) < 2:\n            continue\n        prices_sorted = sorted(prices, key=lambda x: x[1])\n        lowest = prices_sorted[0]\n        highest = prices_sorted[-1]\n        if lowest[1] == 0:\n            continue\n        price_diff_pct = ((highest[1] - lowest[1]) / lowest[1]) * 100\n        if price_diff_pct > 1.8:\n            dashboard_rows.append({\n                'token_name': pairs[0]['token_name'],\n                'token_symbol': pairs[0]['token_symbol'],\n                'token_address': token_addr,\n                'lowest_dex': lowest[0],\n                'lowest_price': lowest[1],\n                'highest_dex': highest[0],\n                'highest_price': highest[1],\n                'price_diff_pct': round(price_diff_pct, 2)\n            })\n    dashboard_rows.sort(key=lambda x: x['price_diff_pct'], reverse=True)\n    return dashboard_rows\n\ndef fetch_pairs_generic(dex_name):\n    # Placeholder                         "import unittest\nfrom unittest.mock import patch, MagicMock\nfrom collections import defaultdict\n\n# Import functions from the code to test\n# (Assume the code above is in the same file or available as module-level functions)\n# We'll import only the functions we need for testing\n\n# Functions to test:\n# - fetch_pairs_generic\n# - fetch_all_dex_pairs\n# - aggregate_token_data\n# - analyze_tokens\n\n# For this test code, we assume the functions are defined in the same namespace.\n# If they were in a module, e.g., monitor.py, you would use:\n# from monitor import fetch_pairs_generic, fetch_all_dex_pairs, aggregate_token_data, analyze_tokens\n\nclass TestDEXMonitor(unittest.TestCase):\n\n    @patch('requests.post')\n    def test_fetch_pairs_generic_success(self, mock_post):\n        # 0]\n        if len(prices) < 2:\n            continue\n        prices_sorted = sorted(prices, key=lambda x: x[1])\n        lowest = prices_sorted[0]\n        highest = prices_sorted[-1]\n        if ''' % TOP_N_PAIRS\n    try:\n        resp = requests.post(endpoint, json={'query': query}, timeout=10)\n        resp.raise_for_status()\n        data = resp.json()['data']['pairs']\n    except difference > 1.8%.\n    \"\"\"\n    dashboard_rows = []\n    for token_addr, pairs in tokens_multi_dex.items():\n        prices = [(pair['dex'], pair['price']) for pair in pairs if pair['price'] > lowest[1] == 0:\n            continue\n        price_diff_pct = ((highest[1] - lowest[1]) / lowest[1]) * 100\n        if price_diff_pct > 1.8:\n            dashboard_rows.append({\n                'token_name': pairs[0]['token_name'],\n                'token_symbol': pairs[0]['token_symbol'],\n                'token_address': token_addr,\n                'lowest_dex': lowest[0],\n                         "import unittest\nfrom unittest.mock import patch, MagicMock\nfrom collections import defaultdict\n\n# Import functions to test from the original code\n# We'll redefine them here for isolation, but in practice, you'd import:\n# from your_module import fetch_pairs_generic, fetch_all_dex_pairs, aggregate_token_data, analyze_tokens\n\n# For the purpose of testing, we redefine the relevant functions with dependency injection\n\nDEX_ENDPOINTS = {\n    'Uniswap': 'https://api.thegraph.com/subgraphs/name/uniswap/uniswap-v2',\n    'PancakeSwap': 'https://bsc.streamingfast.io/subgraphs/name/pancakeswap/exchange-v2',\n    'Sushiswap': 'https://api.thegraph.com/subgraphs/name/sushiswap/exchange',\n}\nTOP_N_PAIRS = 50\n\ndef fetch_pairs_generic(dex_name, requests_post=None):\n    \"\"\"\n    Generic function to fetch token pairs and prices from a DEX using TheGraph.\n    Returns a list of dicts with token info and price.\n    \"\"\"\n    endpoint = DEX_ENDPOINTS[dex_name]\n    query = '''\n    {\n      pairs(first: %d, orderBy: reserveUSD, orderDirection: desc) {\n        id\n        token0 { id symbol name }\n        token1 { id symbol name }\n        reserveUSD\n        token0Price\n        token1Price\n      }\n    }\n    ''' % TOP_N_PAIRS\n    try:\n        # Allow dependency injection for requests.post (for mocking)\n        if requests_post is None:\n            import requests\n            requests_post = requests.post\n        resp = requests_post(endpoint, json={'query': query}, timeout=10)\n        resp.raise_for_status()\n        data = resp.json()['data']['pairs']\n    except Exception as e:\n        return []\n    pairs = []\n    for pair in data:\n        # Use token0 as base, price is token1Price\n        try:\n            price = float(pair['token1Price'])\n        except (TypeError, ValueError):\n            continue\n        pairs.append({\n            'token_address': pair['token0']['id'],\n            'token_symbol': pair['token0']['symbol'],\n            'token_name': pair['token0']['name'],\n            'pair_address': pair['id'],\n            'price': price,\n            'dex': dex_name\n        })\n    return pairs\n\ndef fetch_all_dex_pairs(fetch_pairs_generic_func=None):\n    \"\"\"\n    Fetches pairs from all DEXs and returns a combined list.\n    \"\"\"\n    dex_names = ['Uniswap', 'PancakeSwap', 'Sushiswap']\n    all_pairs = []\n    if fetch_pairs_generic_func is None:\n        fetch_pairs_generic_func = fetch_pairs_generic\n    for dex in dex_names:\n        pairs = fetch_pairs_generic_func(dex)\n        all_pairs.extend(pairs)\n    return all_pairs\n\ndef aggregate_token_data(fetch_all_dex_pairs_func=None):\n    \"\"\"\n    Aggregates tokens by contract address, keeping only those present on at least two DEXs.\n    Returns a dict: {token_address: [pair_info, ...]}\n    \"\"\"\n    if fetch_all_dex_pairs_func is None:\n        fetch_all_dex_pairs_func = fetch_all_dex_pairs\n    all_pairs = fetch_all_dex_pairs_func()\n    tokens = defaultdict(list)\n    for pair in all_pairs:\n        tokens[pair['token_address']].append(pair)\n    # Only keep tokens present on at least two DEXs\n    tokens_multi_dex = {addr: pairs for addr, pairs in tokens.items() if len(pairs) >= 2}\n    return tokens_multi_dex\n\ndef analyze_tokens(tokens_multi_dex):\n    \"\"\"\n    For each token, finds the lowest/highest price across DEXs,\n    calculates price difference %, and returns dashboard rows for tokens\n    with price difference > 1.8%.\n    \"\"\"\n    dashboard_rows = []\n    for token_addr, pairs in tokens_multi_dex.items():\n        prices = [(pair['dex'], pair['price']) for pair in pairs if pair['price'] > 0]\n        if len(prices) < 2:\n            continue\n        prices_sorted = sorted(prices, key=lambda x: x[1])\n        lowest = prices_sorted[0]\n        highest = prices_sorted[-1]\n        if lowest[1] == 0:\n            continue\n        price_diff_pct = ((highest[1] - lowest[1]) / lowest[1]) * 100\n        if price_diff_pct > 1.8:\n            dashboard_rows.append({\n                'token_name': pairs[0]['token_name'],\n                'token_symbol': pairs[0]['token_symbol'],\n                'token_address': token_addr,\n                'lowest_dex': lowest[0],\n                'lowest_price': lowest[1],\n                'highest_dex': highest[0],\n                'highest_price': highest[1],\n                'price_diff_pct': round(price_diff_pct, 2)\n            })\n    dashboard_rows.sort(key=lambda x: x['price_diff_pct'], reverse=True)\n    return dashboard_rows\n\nclass TestDexMonitor(unittest.TestCase):\n\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Example token data for mocking\n        self.mock_pairs = [\n            # Token A on Uniswap and Sushiswap, price diff > 1.8%\n            {'token_address': '0xAAA', 'token_symbol': 'AAA', 'token_name': 'TokenA', 'pair_address': 'pair1', 'price': 1.00, 'dex': 'Uniswap'},\n            {'token_address': '0xAAA', 'token_symbol': 'AAA', 'token_name': 'TokenA', 'pair_address': 'pair2', 'price': 1.05, 'dex': 'Sushiswap'},\n            # Token B on PancakeSwap and Sushiswap, price diff < 1.8%\n            {'token_address': '0xBBB', 'token_symbol': 'BBB', 'token_name': 'TokenB', 'pair_address': 'pair3', 'price': 2.00, 'dex': 'PancakeSwap'},\n            {'token_address': '0xBBB', 'token_symbol': 'BBB', 'token_name': 'TokenB', 'pair_address': 'pair4', 'price': 2.02, 'dex': 'Sushiswap'},\n            # Token C on all 3 DEXs, price diff > 1.8%\n            {'token_address': '0xCCC', 'token_symbol': 'CCC', 'token_name': 'TokenC', 'pair_address': 'pair5', 'price': 10.00, 'dex': 'Uniswap'},\n            {'token_address': '0xCCC', 'token_symbol': 'CCC', 'token_name': 'TokenC', 'pair_address': 'pair6', 'price': 10.30, 'dex': 'PancakeSwap'},\n            {'token_address': '0xCCC', 'token_symbol': 'CCC', 'token_name': 'TokenC', 'pair_address': 'pair7', 'price': 10.10, 'dex': 'Sushiswap'},\n            # Token F on two DEXs, both prices zero (should not appear)\n            {'token_address': '0xFFF', 'token_symbol': 'FFF', 'token_name': 'TokenF', 'pair_address': 'pair11', 'price': 0.00, 'dex': 'Uniswap'},\n            {'token_address': '0xFFF', 'token_symbol': 'FFF', 'token_name': 'TokenF', 'pair_address': 'pair12', 'price': 0.00, 'dex': 'Sushiswap'},\n            # Token G on two DEXs, but one price is negative (should not appear)\n            {'token_address': '0xGGG', 'token_symbol': 'GGG', 'token_name': 'TokenG', 'pair_address': 'pair13', 'price': -1.00, 'dex': 'Uniswap'},\n            {'token_address': '0xGGG', 'token_symbol': 'GGG', 'token_name': 'TokenG', 'pair_address': 'pair14', 'price': 2.00, 'dex': 'Sushiswap'},\n        ]\n\n    def mock_fetch_pairs_generic(self, dex_name):\n        # Return only pairs for the requested dex\n        return [p for p in self.mock_pairs if p['dex'] == dex_name]\n\n    def mock_fetch_all_dex_pairs(self):\n        return self.mock_pairs\n\n    def test_fetch_pairs_generic_success(self):\n        # Mock requests.post to return a controlled response\n        mock_response = MagicMock()\n        mock_response.raise_for_status.return_value = None\n        mock_response.json.return_value = {\n            'data': {\n                'pairs': [\n                    {\n                        'id': 'pair1',\n                        'token0': {'id': '0xAAA', 'symbol': 'AAA', 'name': 'TokenA'},\n                        'token1': {'id': '0xBBB', 'symbol': 'BBB', 'name': 'TokenB'},\n                        'reserveUSD': '1000',\n                        'token0Price': '1.0',\n                        'token1Price': '1.05'\n                    },\n                    {\n                        'id': 'pair2',\n                        'token0': {'id': '0xCCC', 'symbol': 'CCC', 'name': 'TokenC'},\n                        'token1': {'id': '0xDDD', 'symbol': 'DDD', 'name': 'TokenD'},\n                        'reserveUSD': '2000',\n                        'token0Price': '10.0',\n                        'token1Price': '10.3'\n                    }\n                ]\n            }\n        }\n        def mock_post(endpoint, json, timeout):\n            return mock_response\n        pairs = fetch_pairs_generic('Uniswap', requests_post=mock_post)\n        self.assertEqual(len(pairs), 2)\n        self.assertEqual(pairs[0]['token_address'], '0xAAA')\n        self.assertEqual(pairs[0]['price'], 1.05)\n        self.assertEqual(pairs[1]['token_address'], '0xCCC')\n        self.assertEqual(pairs[1]['price'], 10.3)\n\n    def test_fetch_pairs_generic_failure(self):\n        # 'https://api.thegraph.com/subgraphs/name/sushiswap/exchange',\n}\n\n# Number of top pairs to fetch from each DEX\nTOP_N_PAIRS = 50\n\n# Flask app setup\napp = Flask(__name__)\n\n# Shared data structure for dashboard (thread-safe)\ndashboard_data = []\ndashboard_lock = threading.Lock()\n\n# -------------------------------\n# Helper functions for DEX queries\n# -------------------------------\n\ndef fetch_pairs_generic(dex_name):\n    \"\"\"\n    Generic function to fetch token pairs and prices from a DEX using TheGraph.\n    Returns a list of dicts with token info and price.\n    \"\"\"\n    endpoint = DEX_ENDPOINTS[dex_name]\n    query = '''\n    {\n      pairs(first: %d, orderBy: reserveUSD, orderDirection: desc) {\n        id\n        token0 { id symbol name }\n        token1 { id symbol name }\n        reserveUSD\n        token0Price\n        token1Price\n      }\n    }\n    ''' % TOP_N_PAIRS\n    try:\n        resp = requests.post(endpoint, json={'query': query}, timeout=10)\n        resp.raise_for_status()\n        data = resp.json()['data']['pairs']\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"[{dex_name}] Error fetching pairs: {e}\")\n        return []\n    pairs = []\n    for pair in data:\n        # Use token0 as base, price is token1Price\n        try:\n            price = float(pair['token1Price'])\n        except (TypeError, ValueError):\n            continue\n        pairs.append({\n            'token_address': pair['token0']['id'],\n            'token_symbol': pair['token0']['symbol'],\n            'token_name': pair['token0']['name'],\n            'pair_address': pair['id'],\n            'price': price,\n            'dex': dex_name\n        })\n    return pairs\n\ndef fetch_all_dex_pairs():\n = fetch_pairs_generic(dex)\n        all_pairs.extend(pairs)\n    return all_pairs\n\n# -------------------------------\n# Data Aggregation & Analysis\n# -------------------------------\n\ndef the lowest/highest price across DEXs,\n    calculates price difference %, and returns dashboard rows for tokens\n    with price difference > 1.8%.\n    \"\"\"\n    dashboard_rows = []\n    for ((highest[1] - lowest[1]) / lowest[1]) * 100\n        if price_diff_pct > 1.8:\n            dashboard_rows.append({\n                'token_name': pairs[0]['token_name'],\n 'https://api.thegraph.com/subgraphs/name/sushiswap/exchange',\n}\n\nTOP_N_PAIRS = 50\n\ndef fetch_pairs_generic(dex_name):\n    \"\"\"\n    Generic function to fetch token pairs and prices from a DEX using TheGraph.\n    Returns a list of dicts with token info and price.\n    \"\"\"\n    endpoint = DEX_ENDPOINTS[dex_name]\n    query = '''\n    {\n      pairs(first: %d, orderBy: reserveUSD, orderDirection: desc) {\n        id\n        token0 { id symbol name }\n        token1 { id symbol name }\n        reserveUSD\n        token0Price\n        token1Price\n      }\n    }\n    ''' % TOP_N_PAIRS\n    try:\n        import requests\n        resp = requests.post(endpoint, json={'query': query}, timeout=10)\n        resp.raise_for_status()\n        data = resp.json()['data']['pairs']\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"[{dex_name}] Error fetching pairs: {e}\")\n        return []\n    pairs = []\n    for pair in data:\n        try:\n            price = float(pair['token1Price'])\n        except (TypeError, ValueError):\n            continue\n        pairs.append({\n            'token_address': pair['token0']['id'],\n            'token_symbol': pair['token0']['symbol'],\n            'token_name': pair['token0']['name'],\n            'pair_address': pair['id'],\n            'price': price,\n            'dex': dex_name\n        })\n    return pairs\n\ndef fetch_all_dex_pairs():\n    dex_names = ['Uniswap', 'PancakeSwap', 'Sushiswap']\n    all_pairs = []\n    for dex in dex_names:\n        pairs = fetch_pairs_generic(dex)\n        all_pairs.extend(pairs)\n    return all_pairs\n\ndef aggregate_token_data():\n    all_pairs = fetch_all_dex_pairs()\n    tokens = defaultdict(list)\n    for pair in all_pairs:\n        tokens[pair['token_address']].append(pair)\n    tokens_multi_dex = {addr: pairs for addr, pairs in tokens.items() if len(pairs) >= 2}\n    return tokens_multi_dex\n\ndef analyze_tokens(tokens_multi_dex):\n    dashboard_rows = []\n    for token_addr, pairs in tokens_multi_dex.items():\n        prices = [(pair['dex'], pair['price']) for pair in pairs if pair['price'] > 0]\n        if len(prices) < 2:\n            continue\n        prices_sorted = sorted(prices, key=lambda x: x[1])\n        lowest = prices_sorted[0]\n        highest = prices_sorted[-1]\n        if lowest[1] == 0:\n            continue\n        price_diff_pct = ((highest[1] - lowest[1]) / lowest[1]) * 100\n        if price_diff_pct > 1.8:\n            dashboard_rows.append({\n                'token_name': pairs[0]['token_name'],\n                'token_symbol': pairs[0]['token_symbol'],\n                'token_address': token_addr,\n                'lowest_dex': lowest[0],\n                'lowest_price': lowest[1],\n                'highest_dex': highest[0],\n                'highest_price': highest[1],\n                'price_diff_pct': round(price_diff_pct, 2)\n            })\n    dashboard_rows.sort(key=lambda x: x['price_diff_pct'], reverse=True)\n    return dashboard_rows\n\n# --- End: Functions to be tested ---\n\nclass TestDexMonitoring(unittest.TestCase):\n    def
